<script type="text/javascript">
		var previd = '';
		function highlightSection(currid, currsection, focus)
		{
			maxpos = 0;
			var search = $('#search');
			var section = $('#section');

			if(currid == previd)
				return;
			$('#' + currid).css('color', 'white');

			if(previd != '')
			{
				$('#' + previd).css('color', '#3070b0');
				$('#' + previd).css('backgroundColor', '');
				$('#' + previd).css('border', '');
			}

			previd = currid;

			section.val(currsection);
			if(currid == 'section_bluraymovies' || currid == 'section_dvdmovies' || currid == 'section_uvmovies' || currid == 'section_aivmovies' || currid == 'section_itunesmovies' || currid == 'section_3d' || currid == 'section_ps3')
			{
				$('#search_locale').css('display', 'block');
				$('#search_clear').css('left', '452px');
			}
			else
			{
				$('#search_locale').css('display', 'none');
				$('#search_clear').css('left', '488px');
			}

			if(focus)
				search.focus();

			document.cookie = 'search_section='+currsection+'; path=/; domain=.blu-ray.com';
		}
		</script>

		function usepreload()
		{
			if(navigator.userAgent.match(/Kindle/i))
				return(true);

			if(navigator.userAgent.match(/iPhone/i) || navigator.userAgent.match(/iPod/i) || (navigator.userAgent.match(/Android/i) && navigator.userAgent.match(/Mobile/i)) || navigator.userAgent.match(/Mobile Safari/i))
				return(false);

			return(true);
		}

		function ismobile()
		{
//			if(navigator.userAgent.match(/Kindle/i))
//				return(false);

//			if(navigator.userAgent.match(/iPhone/i) || navigator.userAgent.match(/iPod/i) || (navigator.userAgent.match(/Android/i) && navigator.userAgent.match(/Mobile/i)) || navigator.userAgent.match(/Mobile Safari/i))
//				return(true);

			return(false);
		}

		var pos = -1, lastpos = -1, maxpos = -1;
		function highlightSearchOption(newpos)
		{
			if(pos == newpos)
				return;

			$('#match' + pos).removeClass('selected');

			if(newpos < -1)
				newpos = maxpos-1;
			else if(newpos >= maxpos)
				newpos = -1;

			if((newpos >= 0) && (newpos < maxpos))
				$('#match' + newpos).addClass('selected');

			lastpos = pos;
			pos = newpos;
			previewSearchOption();
		}

		var preload1 = new Image();
		var preload2 = new Image();
		function previewSearchOption()
		{
			if(pos < 0)
				imagepos = 0;
			else
				imagepos = pos;

			if(ismobile())
			{
				search_preview.css('display', 'none');
				return;
			}

			if(section.val() == 'theatrical' || section.val() == 'castandcrew' || section.val() == 'uvmovies' || section.val() == 'aivmovies' || section.val() == 'itunesmovies')
			{
				overallrating.html('<div class="product_rating" style="margin-top: -2px; margin-bottom: 6px"><div class="average_rating" style="width:' + Math.ceil(ratings[imagepos] * 10) + '%"></div></div>');
			}
			else
			{
				if(ratings[imagepos] != '')
					overallrating.html('<img src="http://www.blu-ray.com/images/rating/b' + ratings[imagepos] + '.jpg" width="69" height="13" border="0" style="vertical-align: text-bottom; margin-bottom: 5px">');
				else
					overallrating.html('<img src="http://www.blu-ray.com/images/rating/b0.jpg" width="69" height="13" border="0" style="vertical-align: text-bottom; margin-bottom: 5px">');
			}

			if(images[imagepos] != '')
			{
				previewthumb.attr('src', images[imagepos]);
				previewthumb.removeAttr('width');
				previewthumb.removeAttr('height');
			}
			else
			{
				previewthumb.attr('src', 'http://www.blu-ray.com/images/nocover_medium.gif');
				previewthumb.attr('width', '156');
				previewthumb.attr('height', '201');
			}

			if(usepreload())
			{
				if(pos == (lastpos + 1))
				{
					if(images[imagepos + 1] != undefined)
					{
						if(images[imagepos + 1] != '')
							preload1.src = images[imagepos + 1];
						else
							preload1.src = 'http://www.blu-ray.com/images/nocover_medium.gif';
					}

					if(images[imagepos + 2] != undefined)
					{
						if(images[imagepos + 2] != '')
							preload2.src = images[imagepos + 2];
						else
							preload2.src = 'http://www.blu-ray.com/images/nocover_medium.gif';
					}
				}
				else if(pos == (lastpos - 1))
				{
					if(images[imagepos - 1] != undefined)
					{
						if(images[imagepos - 1] != '')
							preload2.src = images[imagepos - 1];
						else
							preload2.src = 'http://www.blu-ray.com/images/nocover_medium.gif';
					}

					if(images[imagepos - 2] != undefined)
					{
						if(images[imagepos - 2] != '')
							preload2.src = images[imagepos - 2];
						else
							preload2.src = 'http://www.blu-ray.com/images/nocover_medium.gif';
					}
				}
				else
				{
					if(images[imagepos + 1] != undefined)
					{
						if(images[imagepos + 1] != '')
							preload2.src = images[imagepos + 1];
						else
							preload2.src = 'http://www.blu-ray.com/images/nocover_medium.gif';
					}

					if(images[imagepos - 1] != undefined)
					{
						if(images[imagepos - 1] != '')
							preload2.src = images[imagepos - 1];
						else
							preload2.src = 'http://www.blu-ray.com/images/nocover_medium.gif';
					}
				}
			}
		}

		var retry = 0;
		function getSearchOption()
		{
			if(retry > 10)
				return;
			if((pos >= 0) && (pos < maxpos))
			{
				window.location = urls[pos];
			}
			else
			{
				$('#quicksearch_keyword').val(search.val());
				$('#quicksearch_country').val(quicksearchcountry.val());
				$('#quicksearch_form').submit();
			}
		}

		function tabSearchOption()
		{
			if(retry > 10)
				return;

			if(seqrecv < seqsent)
			{
				retry++;
				setTimeout('tabSearchOption()', 100);
				return;
			}

			if(pos > 0)
				window.location = urls[pos];
			else
				window.location = urls[0];
		}

		var xhr = null;
		var seqsent = 0;
		var seqrecv = 0;
		var aborts = 0;
		function abortSearch()
		{
		}

		var nosearch = 0;
		function searchKeyword()
		{
			if(section.val() != 'bluraymovies' && section.val() != '3d' && section.val() != 'dvdmovies' && section.val() != 'uvmovies' && section.val() != 'aivmovies' && section.val() != 'itunesmovies' && section.val() != 'theatrical' && section.val() != 'castandcrew' && section.val() != 'ps3')
				return;

			if(search.val() != '')
				search_clear.css('display', 'block');
			else
				search_clear.css('display', 'none');

			var seq = ++seqsent;
			xhr = $.post('http://www.blu-ray.com/search/quicksearch.php', { section: section.val(), userid: "-1", country: quicksearchcountry.val(), keyword: search.val() }, function(data) { if(data != '') { if(seq > seqrecv) { seqrecv = seq; highlightSearchOption(-1); search_auto_complete.html(data); search_auto_complete.css('display', 'block'); if(!ismobile() && !nosearch) { search_preview.css('display', 'block'); }} } else { maxpos = -1; search_auto_complete.css('display', 'none'); search_preview.css('display', 'none') }});
		}

		$(document).ready(function()
		{
			window.hovertime = 0;
			window.blurtimer = null;
			window.cancelBlur = false;	// ie fix
			window.cancelKeypress = false; // opera fix

			search.bind('keydown', function(e) { code = e.keyCode ? e.keyCode : e.which; cancelKeypress = false; if(code.toString() == 8 || code.toString() == 32 || code.toString() > 40) { abortSearch(); setTimeout('searchKeyword()', 0) } else if(code.toString() == 9) { tabSearchOption(); } else if(code.toString() == 27) { setTimeout(function() { highlightSearchOption(-1); $('#search_auto_complete').css('display', 'none'); search_preview.css('display', 'none'); search.blur(); }); } else if(code.toString() == 13) { getSearchOption(); e.preventDefault(); cancelKeypress = true; return false; } else if(code.toString() == 38) { highlightSearchOption(pos-1); e.preventDefault(); cancelKeypress = true; return false } else if(code.toString() == 40) { highlightSearchOption(pos+1); e.preventDefault(); return false };});
			search.bind('keypress', function(e) { if(cancelKeypress) { return false; }});
			search.bind('focus', function() { setTimeout(function() { if(maxpos > 0) { $('#search_auto_complete').css('display', 'block'); if(!ismobile()) { search_preview.css('display', 'block'); }} else { searchKeyword() } }, 100); });
			// catch link clicks (uses clicktime and hovertime to allow hovering on an iPad)
			$(document).bind('mousedown', function(e) { var clicktime = (new Date).getTime(); if(e.target.id.slice(0,5) == 'match') { if((clicktime - hovertime) > 50 || (lastpos < 0 && pos == 0)) { getSearchOption(); return false; }} else if(e.target.id == 'search' || e.target.id == 'country_us' || e.target.id == 'country_uk' || e.target.id == 'country_ca' || e.target.id == 'country_de' || e.target.id == 'country_fr' || e.target.id == 'country_au' || e.target.id == 'country_hk' || e.target.id == 'addcollectionlink' || e.target.id == 'addwishlistlink' || e.target.id == 'dvd_addcollectionlink' || e.target.id == 'dvd_addwishlistlink' || e.target.id == 'uv_addcollectionlink' || e.target.id == 'uv_addwishlistlink' || e.target.id == 'aiv_addcollectionlink' || e.target.id == 'aiv_addwishlistlink' || e.target.id == 'itunes_addcollectionlink' || e.target.id == 'itunes_addwishlistlink' || e.target.id == 'ps3_addcollectionlink' || e.target.id == 'ps3_addwishlistlink' || e.target.id == 'addtheatricallink' || e.target.id == 'removecollectionlink' || e.target.id == 'removewishlistlink' || e.target.id == 'dvd_removecollectionlink' || e.target.id == 'dvd_removewishlistlink' || e.target.id == 'uv_removecollectionlink' || e.target.id == 'uv_removewishlistlink' || e.target.id == 'aiv_removecollectionlink' || e.target.id == 'aiv_removewishlistlink' || e.target.id == 'itunes_removecollectionlink' || e.target.id == 'itunes_removewishlistlink' || e.target.id == 'removetheatricallink') { e.returnValue = false; } else { /* $('#debug').append('node: ' + e.target.nodeName + ', id: ' + e.target.id + '<br>'); */ setTimeout(function() { highlightSearchOption(-1); search_auto_complete.css('display', 'none'); search_preview.css('display', 'none'); }, 100); }});
			$('#previewthumb').bind('mousedown', function(e) { if(pos < 0) pos = 0; getSearchOption(); return false; });

			window.userid = -1;

			if(userid > 0)
			{
				addcollectionlink.bind('mouseup', function(e) { search.focus(); if(e.which == 1) { var addpos = (pos > 0) ? pos : 0; $.ajax({url: 'http://www.blu-ray.com/community/collection.php?action=quickadd&u=-1&categoryid=7&addeddevice=2&typeid=1&productid=' + ids[addpos], dataType: 'jsonp'}); collections[addpos] = '1'; addcollection.css('display', 'none'); addwishlist.css('display', 'none'); addother.css('display', 'none'); removecollection.css('display', 'inline'); removewishlist.css('display', 'none'); }; e.preventDefault ? e.preventDefault() : e.returnValue = false; });
				addwishlistlink.bind('mouseup', function(e) { cancelBlur = true; if(e.which == 1) { var addpos = (pos > 0) ? pos : 0; $.ajax({url: 'http://www.blu-ray.com/community/collection.php?action=quickadd&u=-1&categoryid=7&addeddevice=2&typeid=5&productid=' + ids[addpos], dataType: 'jsonp'}); collections[addpos] = '5'; addcollection.css('display', 'none'); addwishlist.css('display', 'none'); addother.css('display', 'none'); removecollection.css('display', 'none'); removewishlist.css('display', 'inline'); }; e.preventDefault ? e.preventDefault() : e.returnValue = false; });
				removecollectionlink.bind('mouseup', function(e) { search.focus(); if(e.which == 1) { var removepos = (pos > 0) ? pos : 0; $.ajax({url: 'http://www.blu-ray.com/community/collection.php?action=quickdelete&u=-1&categoryid=7&productid=' + ids[removepos], dataType: 'jsonp'}); collections[removepos] = '0'; removecollection.css('display', 'none'); removewishlist.css('display', 'none'); addcollection.css('display', 'inline'); addwishlist.css('display', 'inline'); addother.css('display', 'none'); }; e.preventDefault ? e.preventDefault() : e.returnValue = false; });

<h3>Finding Nemo</h3> (2003)
<br><font style="font-size: 5px"><br/></font>
<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" width="728"><tr>
<td style="padding-right: 2px" width="25%"><img border="0" height="101" src="http://images.static-bluray.com/reviews/7129_1_tn.jpg" width="180"/></td>
<td style="padding-right: 2px" width="25%"><img border="0" height="101" src="http://images4.static-bluray.com/reviews/7129_2_tn.jpg" width="180"/></td>
<td style="padding-right: 2px" width="25%"><img border="0" height="101" src="http://images3.static-bluray.com/reviews/7129_3_tn.jpg" width="180"/></td>
<td style="padding-right: 2px" width="25%"><img border="0" height="101" src="http://images2.static-bluray.com/reviews/7129_4_tn.jpg" width="180"/></td>
</tr></table>
<center><i>Screenshots from <a href="http://www.blu-ray.com/movies/Finding-Nemo-Blu-ray/554/">Finding Nemo Blu-ray</a></i></center><br>
In the colorful and warm tropical waters of the Great Barrier Reef, a Clownfish named Marlin 
lives safe and secluded in a quiet cul-de-sac with his only son, Nemo. Fearful of the ocean 
and its unpredictable risks, he struggles to protect his son. Nemo, like all young fish, is 
eager to explore the mysterious reef. When Nemo is unexpectedly taken far from home and 
thrust into a dentist's office fish tank, Marlin finds himself the unlikely hero on an epic 
journey to rescue his son. In his quest, Marlin is joined by a good Samaritan named Dory, a 
Regal Blue Tang fish with the worst short-term memory and biggest heart in the entire 
ocean. As the two fish continue on their journey, encountering numerous dangers, Dory's 
optimism continually forces Marlin to find the courage to take risks and overcome his fears. 
In doing so, Marlin gains the ability to trust and believe, like Dory, that things will work out 
in the end. Confronting seabirds, sewer systems, and even man himself, father and son's 
fateful separation ends in triumph. And the once-fearful Marlin becomes a true hero in the 
eyes of his son, and the entire ocean.<br><br>Starring: <a href="http://www.blu-ray.com/Albert-Brooks/68056/">Albert Brooks</a><font style="color: #999999">,</font> <a href="http://www.blu-ray.com/Ellen-DeGeneres/68117/">Ellen DeGeneres</a><font style="color: #999999">,</font> <a href="http://www.blu-ray.com/Alexander-Gould/68118/">Alexander Gould</a><font style="color: #999999">,</font> <a href="http://www.blu-ray.com/Willem-Dafoe/65916/">Willem Dafoe</a><font style="color: #999999">,</font> <a href="http://www.blu-ray.com/Brad-Garrett/67673/">Brad Garrett</a><font style="color: #999999">,</font> <a href="http://www.blu-ray.com/Allison-Janney/68959/">Allison Janney</a>
<br>Directors: <a href="http://www.blu-ray.com/Lee-Unkrich/68120/">Lee Unkrich</a><font style="color: #999999">,</font> <a href="http://www.blu-ray.com/Andrew-Stanton/68119/">Andrew Stanton</a>
<br> <font style="font-size: 3px"><br/></font>» <a href="http://www.blu-ray.com/itunes/Finding-Nemo-iTunes/113/#Castandcrew" rel="history">See full cast &amp; crew</a>

<script type="text/javascript">
				var pos = -1, maxpos = -1;
				function highlightOption(newpos)
				{
					if(pos == newpos)
						return;

					$('#listmatch' + pos).removeClass('selected');

					if(newpos < -1)
						newpos = maxpos-1;
					else if(newpos >= maxpos)
						newpos = -1;

					if((newpos >= 0) && (newpos < maxpos))
						$('#listmatch' + newpos).addClass('selected');

					pos = newpos;
				}

				function getOption()
				{
					if((pos >= 0) && (pos < maxpos))
					{
						$('#title').val($('#listmatch' + pos).html());
						$('#psimilar').val($('#listmatchid' + pos).val());
						$('#title_auto_complete').html('');
						$('#title_auto_complete').css('display', 'none');
					}

					pos = -1;
				}

				$(document).ready(function()
				{
					$('#title').bind('keyup', function(e) { code = e.keyCode ? e.keyCode : e.which; if(code.toString() == 8 || code.toString() == 32 || code.toString() > 40) { $.post('/products/ajax.php?action=lookupsimilar', { title: $('#title').val() }, function(data) { if(data != '') { highlightOption(-1); $('#title_auto_complete').html(data); $('#title_auto_complete').css('display', 'block'); } else { maxpos = -1; $('#title_auto_complete').css('display', 'none'); }}); }});
					$('#title').bind('keydown', function(e) { code = e.keyCode ? e.keyCode : e.which; if(code.toString() == 9 || code.toString() == 13) { getOption(); } else if(code.toString() == 38) { highlightOption(pos-1); } else if(code.toString() == 40) { highlightOption(pos+1); }});
					$('#title_auto_complete').bind('mousedown', function() { getOption() });
					$('#title').bind('blur', function() { setTimeout(function() { highlightOption(-1); $('#title_auto_complete').html(''); $('#title_auto_complete').css('display', 'none')}, 100); });
				});
				</script>
</td>

<script type="text/javascript">
		$(document).ready(function() {
			$.ajax({
				url: "/inc/scripts/jquery.datetimepicker.js",
				dataType: "script",
				cache: true,
				success: function() {
					$('input[id*="added_datetimepicker_"]').datetimepicker({ 
						format: 'Y-m-d', 
						timepicker: false, 
						closeOnDateSelect: true, 
						allowBlank: true, 
						dayOfWeekStart: 0, 
						maxDate: 0, 
						yearEnd: 2015, 
						scrollInput: false, step: 15 
					});

					$('input[id*="watched_datetimepicker_"]').datetimepicker({ 
						format: 'Y-m-d', 
						timepicker: false, 
						closeOnDateSelect: true, 
						allowBlank: true, 
						dayOfWeekStart: 0, 
						maxDate: 0, 
						yearEnd: 2015, 
						scrollInput: false, step: 15 
					});     
				}
			});
		});
		</script>
<script type="text/javascript">
var Collectable = {
	selctypeid: 0,
	data: {},
	processButtonClick: function(gpid, ctypeid)
	{
		$('#collectablepopup_statusmsg').css('color', '#000').html('');
		Collectable.selctypeid = ctypeid || 0;
		Collectable.data = { gpid: gpid };
		var pop = $('#collectablepopup');
		if(pop.is(':visible'))
		{
			pop.hide();
		}
		else
		{
			$('#collectablepopup_statusmsg').css('color', '#000').html('Loading...');
			$('#collectableform').hide();
			var ui = $('#collectablepopup #coll_ui');
//			var x = Math.max(0, (($(window).width() - ui.innerWidth()) / 2) + $(window).scrollLeft() - $(window).pageXOffset);
//			var y = Math.max(0, (($(window).height() - ui.innerHeight()) / 2) + $(window).scrollTop() - $(window).pageYOffset);
//			ui.css({ left: x + 'px', top: y + 'px'});
			ui.css({ "position": "absolute", "left": "50%", "top": "50%", "margin-top": "-10px", "margin-left": "-10px"})
			var docheight = Math.max($(document).height(), $(window).height());
                        pop.css({ height: docheight + 'px'});
			pop.show();
			var userid = 0;
			$.ajax({
				type:'GET', url:'http://www.blu-ray.com/community/collection.php', dataType:'json', cache:false, timeout:30000, 
				data: { action: 'properties', p: gpid, u: userid },
				success: Collectable.handlePropertiesSuccess,
				error: Collectable.handleActionError
			});
		}
	},
	setWatchedButtonOn: function(action)
	{
                var e = document.getElementById(action + '1');
                if(e.className == 'actions not ' + action)
                {
			e.className = 'actions  ' + action;
                        //e.innerHTML = parseInt(e.innerHTML) + 1;
                        var tooltip = e.parentNode.getAttribute('tooltip');
                        if(tooltip.substring(0, 6) == "Add to")
                                e.parentNode.setAttribute('tooltip', tooltip.replace('Add to ', 'Remove from '));
                }
        },
	setWatchedButtonOff: function(action)
	{ 
		var e = document.getElementById(action + '1');			
		if (e.className == 'actions  ' + action) 
		{
			e.className = 'actions not ' + action;
			//e.innerHTML = parseInt(e.innerHTML) - 1;
			var tooltip = e.parentNode.getAttribute('tooltip');
			if(tooltip.substring(0, 6) == "Remove")
				e.parentNode.setAttribute('tooltip', tooltip.replace('Remove from ', 'Add to '));
		}
	},
	setTheatricalWatchedByCtypeid: function(ctypeid)
	{
		// set all off
		var actions = ['watched', 'watchlist', 'notinterested'];
                for(var i=0; i<actions.length; i++)
                {
			Collectable.setWatchedButtonOff(actions[i]);
                }
		// Highlight button for the chosen system category if any.
		if (ctypeid == 11138) {
			Collectable.setWatchedButtonOn('watched');
		} else if (ctypeid == 54989) {
			Collectable.setWatchedButtonOn('watchlist');
		} else if (ctypeid == 17558) {
			Collectable.setWatchedButtonOn('notinterested');
		}
	},
	handleActionSuccess: function(data, textStatus, jqXHR)
	{
		$('#popupformbuttons').show();
		if(data && 'status' in data && 'action' in data)
		{
			var collpopbuttontitle = 'Add to collection';
			if(Collectable.data.categoryid == 20)
			{
				collpopbuttontitle = "Seen in theater";
			}
			if(data.action == "add")
			{
				$('#collectableform input[name=collectionid_0]').val(data.cid);
				$('#collectableform input[name=action]').val('multiedit');
				$('#collectableform input[name=submit]').val('Update collection');
				collpopbuttontitle = 'In your ' + data.ctype + ' collection';
				if (Collectable.data.categoryid == 20) {
					Collectable.setTheatricalWatchedByCtypeid(data.ctypeid);
					collpopbuttontitle = 'In your collection';
					if (data.seenintheater == 1)
						collpopbuttontitle = "You've seen it in theaters";
				}
				$('#collectableform div[id=coll_delete]').show();

			}
			else if (data.action == "multiedit")
			{
				$('#collectableform input[name=action]').val('multiedit');
				$('#collectableform input[name=submit]').val('Update collection');
				collpopbuttontitle = 'In your ' + data.ctype + ' collection';
				if (Collectable.data.categoryid == 20) {
					Collectable.setTheatricalWatchedByCtypeid(data.ctypeid);
					collpopbuttontitle = 'In your collection';
					if (data.seenintheater == 1)
						collpopbuttontitle = "You've seen it in theaters";
				}
				$('#collectableform div[id=coll_delete]').show();
			}
			else if (data.action == "multidelete")
			{
				$('#collectableform input[name=collectionid_0]').val('');
				$('#collectableform input[name=action]').val('add');
				$('#collectableform input[name=submit]').val('Add to collection');
				collpopbuttontitle = 'Add to collection';
				if(Collectable.data.categoryid == 20)
				{
					Collectable.setTheatricalWatchedByCtypeid(0);
					collpopbuttontitle = "Seen in theater";
				}
				$('#collectableform div[id=coll_delete]').hide();
			}
			$('#collectablepopupbutton_' + Collectable.data.gpid).find('a').html(collpopbuttontitle);
			$('#collectablepopup_statusmsg').css('color', '#000').html('');
			$('#collectablepopup').hide();
		}
		else
		{
			var msg = '';
			if(data && 'error' in data)
				msg = 'Failed: ' + data.error;
			else
				msg = 'Failed: Unknown error';

			$('#collectablepopup_statusmsg').css('color', '#f00').html(msg);
		}
	},
	handleActionError: function(jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown)
	{
		var msg = 'Failed: (' + textStatus+') ' + errorThrown;
		$('#collectablepopup_statusmsg').css('color', '#f00').html(msg);
		$('#popupformbuttons').show();
	},
	handlePropertiesSuccess: function(data, textStatus, jqXHR)
	{
		if(data && 'status' in data && data.status == 1 && 'action' in data && data.action == "properties")
		{
			$('#collectablepopup_statusmsg').css('color', '#000').html('');
			var form = $('#collectableform');
			form.show();
			$('#popupformbuttons').show();
			var userid = 0;
			var gpid = data.p.gpid;
			var title = data.p.title;
			var editmode = data.incoll > 0;
			Collectable.data = { gpid: gpid, categoryid: data.p.categoryid };

			form.find('tr[id=retailer_row]').hide();
			if(Collectable.data.categoryid != 20)
				form.find('tr[id=retailer_row]').show();

			var ratingbubble = form.find('#ratingbubble');
			ratingbubble.hide();
			ratingbubble.load('http://www.blu-ray.com/community/ratings.php?action=ratingwidget&p='+gpid+' #ratingwidget', function(response, status, xhr)
			{
				if(status != "error")
					ratingbubble.show();
			});

			var typeidselect = '';
			var selid = 0;
			for(var i=0; i<data.ctypes.length; ++i)
			{
				var ctype = data.ctypes[i];
				var sel = '';
				if(ctype.sel == 1)
					selid = ctype.id;
				var option = '<option value="' + ctype.id + '">' + ctype.name + '</option>';
				typeidselect += option;
			}
			if(Collectable.selctypeid > 0)
				selid = Collectable.selctypeid;
			form.find('select[name=typeid_0]').html(typeidselect);		
			form.find('select[name=typeid_0] option').prop('selected', false);
			form.find('select[name=typeid_0]').find('option[value='+selid+']').prop('selected', true);

			var selid = 0;
			var retaileridselect = '<option value="-1"></option>';
			for(var i=0; i<data.retailers.length; ++i)
			{
				var retailer = data.retailers[i];
				var sel = '';
				if(retailer.sel == 1)
					selid = retailer.id;
				var option = '<option value="' + retailer.id + '">' + retailer.name + '</option>';
				retaileridselect += option;
			}
//			if(Collectable.selctypeid > 0)
//				selid = Collectable.selctypeid;
			form.find('select[name=retailerid_0]').html(retaileridselect);
			form.find('select[name=retailerid_0] option').prop('selected', false);
			form.find('select[name=retailerid_0]').find('option[value='+selid+']').prop('selected', true);

			form.find('a[id=addcustomcategory]').prop('href', 'http://www.blu-ray.com/community/collection.php?u='+userid+'&action=managecategories&categoryid='+data.p.categoryid);
			form.find('input[name=productid]').val(data.p.id);
			form.find('input[name=categoryid]').val(data.p.categoryid);
			form.find('img.coverimg').attr('src', data.p.coverurl);
			form.find('input[name=added_datetimepicker_0]').val(data.c.addeddate);
			form.find('div[id=watched_label]').html(data.p.isgame == 1 ? "Played" : "Watched");
			form.find('input[name=watched_0]').prop('checked', data.c.watched == 1 ? true: false);
			if(data.c.watched == 1)
				form.find('div[id=divwatchedtimestamp_0]').show();
			else
				form.find('div[id=divwatchedtimestamp_0]').hide();
			form.find('input[name=watched_datetimepicker_0]').val(data.c.watcheddate);
			form.find('input[name=rewatched_datetimepicker_0]').val(data.c.rewatcheddate);
			if(data.p.categoryid == 20)
			{
				form.find('input[name=seenintheater_0]').prop('checked', data.c.seenintheater == 1 ? true: false);
				form.find('tr[id=seenintheater_row]').show();
				if(Collectable.selctypeid == 54989 || Collectable.selctypeid == 17558)
				{
					// uncheck these for watchlist and notinterested
					if(data.c.watched != 1)
					{
						form.find('input[name=watched_0]').prop('checked', false);
						form.find('div[id=divwatchedtimestamp_0]').hide();
						form.find('input[name=seenintheater_0]').prop('checked', false);
					}
				}
				else if(Collectable.selctypeid == 11138)
				{
					// Uncheck seenintheater for watched
					//form.find('input[name=seenintheater_0]').prop('checked', false);
					// Check wathced cb
					form.find('input[name=watched_0]').prop('checked', true);
					form.find('div[id=divwatchedtimestamp_0]').show();
					if(!data.c.watcheddate && !editmode)
						form.find('input[name=watched_datetimepicker_0]').val('2015-02-24');
				}
			}
			else
			{
				form.find('tr[id=seenintheater_row]').hide();
			}
			form.find('textarea[name=description_0]').html(data.c.comment);
			if (data.c.price > 0)
				form.find('input[name=price_0]').val(data.c.price / 100);
			else
				form.find('input[name=price_0]').val('');
			form.find('input[name=pricecomment_0]').val(data.c.pricecomment);
			form.find('input[name=exclude_0]').prop('checked', data.c.exclude == 1 ? true: false);
			form.find('input[name=collectionid_0]').val(data.c.cid);
			if (editmode) {
				form.find('input[name=action]').val('multiedit');
				form.find('input[name=submit]').val('Update collection');
				form.find('div[id=coll_delete]').show();
				var collpopbuttontitle = 'In your ' + data.c.type + ' collection';
				if (data.p.categoryid == 20) {
					Collectable.setTheatricalWatchedByCtypeid(data.c.typeid);
					collpopbuttontitle = 'In your collection';
					if (data.c.seenintheater == 1)
						collpopbuttontitle = "You've seen it in theaters";
				}
				$('#collectablepopupbutton_' + gpid).find('a').html(collpopbuttontitle);
			} else {
				form.find('input[name=action]').val('add');
				form.find('input[name=submit]').val('Add to collection');
				form.find('div[id=coll_delete]').hide();
				var collpopbuttontitle = 'Add to collection';
				if (data.p.categoryid == 20)
					collpopbuttontitle = 'Seen in theater';
				$('#collectablepopupbutton_' + gpid).find('a').html(collpopbuttontitle);
			}
			var ui = $('#collectablepopup #coll_ui');
			var x = Math.max(0, (($(window).width() - ui.outerWidth()) / 2) + $(window).scrollLeft());
			var y = Math.max(0, (($(window).height() - ui.outerHeight()) / 2) + $(window).scrollTop());
			ui.css({ left: x + 'px', top: y + 'px'});
		} else {
			var msg = '';
			if (data && 'error' in data) {
				msg = 'Failed: ' + data.error;
			} else {
				msg = 'Failed: Unknown error';
			}
			$('#collectablepopup_statusmsg').css('color', '#f00').html(msg);
		}
	}
}
$(document).ready(function() {
	$('#collectableform').on('submit', function(e) {
		e.preventDefault();
		$('#popupformbuttons').hide();
		var action = $('#collectableform input[name=action]').val();
		if (action == "add") {
			$('#collectablepopup_statusmsg').css('color', '#000').html('Adding...');
		} else if (action == "multiedit") {
			$('#collectablepopup_statusmsg').css('color', '#000').html('Updating...');
		}
		var data = $('#collectableform').serialize();
		$.ajax({
			type:'POST', url:'http://www.blu-ray.com/community/collection.php', dataType:'json', cache:false, timeout:30000, 
			processData:false, data: data,
			success: Collectable.handleActionSuccess,
			error: Collectable.handleActionError
		});
	});
	$('#collectableform div[id=coll_delete]').on('click', function(e) {
		e.preventDefault();
		$('#popupformbuttons').hide();
		var cid =  $('#collectableform input[name=collectionid_0]').val();
		var categoryid =  $('#collectableform input[name=categoryid]').val();
		var userid =  $('#collectableform input[name=u]').val();
		$('#collectablepopup_statusmsg').css('color', '#000').html('Deleting...');
		$.ajax({
			type:'GET', url:'http://www.blu-ray.com/community/collection.php', dataType:'json', cache:false, timeout:30000, 
			data: { action: 'multidelete', checkbox0: cid, ajax: 1, u: userid, categoryid: categoryid },
			success: Collectable.handleActionSuccess,
			error: Collectable.handleActionError
		});
	});
	$('#collectablepopup').on('click', function(e) {
		var popupui = $(this).find('#coll_ui');
		if (!popupui.is(e.target) && popupui.has(e.target).length === 0) {
			// if the target of the click isn't the popup nor a descendant of the popup, then hide the popup
			$(this).hide();
		}
	});
        $('#collectablepopup.popup').on('escapePopupEvent', function(e) {
		$('#collectablepopup').hide();
	});
	$(document).on( 'keydown', function ( e ) {
                if ( e.keyCode === 27 ) {
                        $('.popup').trigger('escapePopupEvent');
                }
        });	
});
</script>
<style type="text/css">
#pricetrackpopup {
	position:absolute;
	display:none;
	top:0;
	left:0;
	width:100%;
	height:100%;
	background-color:transparent;
	font-style:normal;
}
#pricetrackpopup #prtr_ui {
	position:absolute;
	padding:15px;
	width:630px;
	background-color:#f7fafd; 
	border: 1px solid #bbb;
        -webkit-border-radius: 4px;
        -moz-border-radius: 4px;

<script type="text/javascript">
	var pricetracked = {};
	function processPricetrackButtonClick(gpid, trid) {
		$('#pricetrackpopup_statusmsg').css('color', '#000').html('');
		pricetracked = { gpid: gpid, trid: trid };
		var pop = $('#pricetrackpopup');
		if (pop.is(':visible')) {
			pop.hide();
		} else {
			$('#pricetrackpopup_statusmsg').css('color', '#000').html('Loading...');
			$('#pricetrackform').hide();
			var ui = $('#pricetrackpopup #prtr_ui');
			var x = Math.max(0, (($(window).width() - ui.outerWidth()) / 2) + $(window).scrollLeft());
			var y = Math.max(0, (($(window).height() - ui.outerHeight()) / 2) + $(window).scrollTop());
			ui.css({ left: x + 'px', top: y + 'px'});
			pop.show();
			var docheight = Math.max($(document).height(), $(window).height());
                        pop.css({ height: docheight + 'px'});
			var qdata = { action: 'properties', p: gpid };
			if (trid > 0) {
				qdata['id'] = trid;
			}
			$.ajax({
				type:'GET', url:'http://www.blu-ray.com/community/pricetracker.php', dataType:'json', cache:false, timeout:30000, 
				data: qdata,
				success: handlePricetrackPropertiesSuccess,
				error: handlePricetrackActionError
			});
		}

	};
	var handlePricetrackActionSuccess = function(data, textStatus, jqXHR) {
		$('#pricetrackformbuttons').show();
		if (data && 'status' in data && 'action' in data) {
			var form = $('#pricetrackform');
			var currency = form.find('div[id=prtr_retailers]').find('div.currency').first().html();
			var popupbuttontitle = 'Set price tracking';
			if (data.action == "add") {
				var tr = data.tr[0]; // pick first if more than 1
				form.find('input[name=id]').val(tr.trid);
				form.find('input[name=action]').val('edit');
				form.find('input[name=submit]').val('Update tracking');
				popupbuttontitle = 'Edit price target: '+currency+tr.myprice+' + '+currency+tr.myrange;
				form.find('div[id=prtr_delete]').show();

			} else if (data.action == "edit") {
				var tr = data.tr;
				form.find('input[name=action]').val('edit');
				form.find('input[name=submit]').val('Update tracking');
				popupbuttontitle = 'Edit price target: '+currency+tr.myprice+' + '+currency+tr.myrange;
				form.find('div[id=prtr_delete]').show();
			} else if (data.action == "delete") {
				form.find('input[name=id]').val('');
				form.find('input[name=action]').val('add');
				form.find('input[name=submit]').val('Track');
				popupbuttontitle = 'Set price tracking';
				form.find('div[id=prtr_delete]').hide();
			}
			$('#pricetrackpopupbutton_' + pricetracked.gpid).find('a').html(popupbuttontitle);
			$('#pricetrackpopup_statusmsg').css('color', '#000').html('');
			$('#pricetrackpopup').hide();
		} else {
			var msg = '';
			if (data && 'error' in data) {
				msg = 'Failed: ' + data.error;
			} else {
				msg = 'Failed: Unknown error';
			}
			$('#pricetrackpopup_statusmsg').css('color', '#f00').html(msg);
		}
	};
	var handlePricetrackActionError = function(jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown) {
		var msg = 'Failed: (' + textStatus+') ' + errorThrown;
		$('#pricetrackpopup_statusmsg').css('color', '#f00').html(msg);
		$('#pricetrackformbuttons').show();
	}; 
	var handlePricetrackPropertiesSuccess = function(data, textStatus, jqXHR) {
		if (data && 'status' in data && data.status==1 && 'action' in data && data.action == "properties") {
			$('#pricetrackpopup_statusmsg').css('color', '#000').html('');
			var form = $('#pricetrackform');
			form.show();
			$('#pricetrackformbuttons').show();
			var gpid = data.p.gpid;
			var title = data.p.title;
			var currency = data.p.currency;
			var editmode = data.istr > 0;
			pricetracked = { gpid: gpid };
		
	
			form.find('div[id=prtr_retailers]').empty();
			var tmpl = form.find('div[id=prtr_template]'); 
			tmpl.find('div.currency').html(currency);
			var tmplhtml = tmpl.html();

			var numrets = data.tr.length;
			if (editmode) { 
				numrets = 1;
			}
			for (var i=0; i<numrets; ++i) {
				var tr = data.tr[i];
				var trid = tr.trid;
				var retailerid = tr.retailerid || 1;
				var graphurl = tr.graphurl || "http://images3.static-bluray.com/white.gif";
				var price = tr.price || 0;
				var myprice = tr.myprice || "";
				var myrange = tr.myrange || 0;
				var expire = tr.expire || 8;
				var currentprice = currency + price;
				if (price <= 0) {
					currentprice = "n/a";
				}

				form.find('div[id=prtr_retailers]').append('<div id="prtr_retailer_'+retailerid+'">'+tmplhtml+'</div>');
			
				var retdiv = form.find('div[id=prtr_retailers]').find('#prtr_retailer_'+retailerid);

				retdiv.find('div.currency').html(currency);
				retdiv.find('.currentprice').html(currentprice);
				retdiv.find('input[id=myprice]').val(myprice);
				retdiv.find('input[id=mypricerange]').val(myrange);
				retdiv.find('select[id=myexpire] option').prop('selected', false);
				retdiv.find('select[id=myexpire]').find('option[value='+expire+']').prop('selected', true);
				retdiv.find('img.pricegraphimg').attr('title', title).attr('src', graphurl);

				if (editmode) {
					retdiv.find('input[id=myprice]').attr('name', 'price');
					retdiv.find('input[id=mypricerange]').attr('name', 'pricerange');
					retdiv.find('select[id=myexpire]').attr('name', 'expire');
				} else {
					retdiv.find('input[id=myprice]').attr('name', 'price_'+retailerid);
					retdiv.find('input[id=mypricerange]').attr('name', 'pricerange_'+retailerid);
					retdiv.find('select[id=myexpire]').attr('name', 'expire_'+retailerid);
				}
			}

			if (editmode) {
				form.find('#appstorewidget').hide();
				form.find('input[name=id]').val(trid);
				form.find('input[name=action]').val('edit');
				form.find('input[name=submit]').val('Update tracking');
				form.find('div[id=prtr_delete]').show();
				popupbuttontitle = 'Edit price target: '+currency+myprice+' + '+currency+myrange;
				$('#pricetrackpopupbutton_' + gpid).find('a').html(popupbuttontitle);
			} else {
				form.find('#appstorewidget').show();
				form.find('input[name=p]').val(gpid);
				form.find('input[name=action]').val('add');
				form.find('input[name=submit]').val('Track');
				form.find('div[id=prtr_delete]').hide();
				var popupbuttontitle = 'Set price tracking';
				$('#pricetrackpopupbutton_' + gpid).find('a').html(popupbuttontitle);
			}
			var ui = $('#pricetrackpopup #prtr_ui');
			var x = Math.max(0, (($(window).width() - ui.outerWidth()) / 2) + $(window).scrollLeft());
			var y = Math.max(0, (($(window).height() - ui.outerHeight()) / 2) + $(window).scrollTop());
			ui.css({ left: x + 'px', top: y + 'px'});
		} else {
			var msg = '';
			if (data && 'error' in data) {
				msg = 'Failed: ' + data.error;
			} else {
				msg = 'Failed: Unknown error';
			}
			$('#pricetrackpopup_statusmsg').css('color', '#f00').html(msg);
		}
	};
$(document).ready(function() {
	$('#pricetrackform').on('submit', function(e) {
		e.preventDefault();
		$('#pricetrackformbuttons').hide();
		var action = $('#pricetrackform input[name=action]').val();
		if (action == "add") {
			$('#pricetrackpopup_statusmsg').css('color', '#000').html('Tracking...');
		} else if (action == "edit") {
			$('#pricetrackpopup_statusmsg').css('color', '#000').html('Updating...');
		}
		var data = $('#pricetrackform').serialize();
		$.ajax({
			type:'POST', url:'http://www.blu-ray.com/community/pricetracker.php', dataType:'json', cache:false, timeout:30000, 
			processData:false, data: data,
			success: handlePricetrackActionSuccess,
			error: handlePricetrackActionError
		});
	});
	$('#pricetrackform div[id=prtr_delete]').on('click', function(e) {
		e.preventDefault();
		$('#pricetrackformbuttons').hide();
		var trid =  $('#pricetrackform input[name=id]').val();
		$('#pricetrackpopup_statusmsg').css('color', '#000').html('Removing...');
		$.ajax({
			type:'GET', url:'http://www.blu-ray.com/community/pricetracker.php', dataType:'json', cache:false, timeout:30000, 
			data: { action: 'delete', id: trid, ajax: 1 },
			success: handlePricetrackActionSuccess,
			error: handlePricetrackActionError
		});
	});
	$('#pricetrackpopup').on('click', function(e) {
		var popupui = $(this).find('#prtr_ui');
		if (!popupui.is(e.target) && popupui.has(e.target).length === 0) {
			// if the target of the click isn't the popup nor a descendant of the popup, then hide the popup
			$(this).hide();
		}
	});
        $('#pricetrackpopup.popup').on('escapePopupEvent', function(e) {
                $('#pricetrackpopup').hide();
        });
        $(document).on( 'keydown', function ( e ) {
                if ( e.keyCode === 27 ) {
                        $('.popup').trigger('escapePopupEvent');
                }
        });   	
});
</script>
<script type="text/javascript">

		$(document).ready(function()
		{
			// Initialize history plugin.
			// The callback is called at once by present location.hash. 
			$.historyInit(showTab, 'http://www.blu-ray.com/itunes/Finding-Nemo-iTunes/113/');
		
			// set onclick event for buttons
			$("a[rel='history']").click(function()
			{
				var hash = this.href;
				hash = hash.replace(/^.*#/, '');

				if((window.location.hash == '#'+hash) || (window.location.hash == hash))
					return false;

				// moves to a new page. 
				// pageload is called at once. 
				// hash don't contain "#", "?"
				$.historyLoad(hash);

				return false;
			});

			$(window).bind('hashchange', function() { showTab(window.location.hash) });
			showTab(window.location.hash);
		});

		</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
var ad_offset = 250;
$(document).ready(function()
{
	$.fn.scrollFixed = function(params)
	{
		params = $.extend( {appearAfterDiv: 0, hideBeforeDiv: 0}, params);
		var element = $(this);

		if(params.appearAfterDiv)
			var distanceTop = element.offset().top + $(params.appearAfterDiv).outerHeight(true) + element.outerHeight(true) + ad_offset - 5;
		else
			var distanceTop = element.offset().top + ad_offset - 5;

		if(params.hideBeforeDiv)
			var bottom = $(params.hideBeforeDiv).offset().top - element.outerHeight(true) - 10;
		else
			var bottom = 200000;

		$(window).scroll(function()
		{
			var scrollTop = $(window).scrollTop();

			if(scrollTop > distanceTop && scrollTop < bottom)
				element.css({'position':'fixed', 'top':'5px'});
			else
				element.css({'position':'static'});
		});
	};
});
</script>
